## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="1d146-1613">Commenti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d146-1613">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1d146-1614">La classe **MS-DFSR-LocalSettings** fa parte del supporto del servizio Replica DFS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d146-1614">The **ms-DFSR-LocalSettings** class is a part of the DFS Replication service support.</span></span>
